1	MULTI-NATIONAL	\N	 samples that were designed to maximize measures of heterogeneity or sample human diversity in a global fashion. Examples OEFNER|GLOBAL and CEPH repository.
2	NORTH/EAST AFRICA & MIDDLE EAST	\N	 samples collected from North Africa (including Sahara desert), East Africa (south to Equator), Levant, Persian Gulf.
3	WEST AFRICA	\N	 Sub-Saharan Nations bordering Atlantic north of Congo River, and Central/Southern Atlantic Island Nations.
4	CENTRAL/SOUTH AFRICA	\N	 Nations south of Equator, Madagascar & neighboring Island Nations.
5	EUROPE	\N	 Samples from Europe north and west of Caucasus Mountains, Scandinavia, Atlantic Islands.
6	EAST ASIA	\N	 Samples from Eastern and South Eastern Mainland Asia, Northern Pacific Island Nations.
7	PACIFIC	\N	 Samples from Australia, New Zealand, Central and Southern Pacific Islands, Southeast Asian Peninsular/Island Nations.
8	CENTRAL ASIA	\N	 Samples from Russia and satellite Republics, Nations bordering Indian Ocean between East Asia and Persian Gulf regions.
9	NORTH AMERICA	\N	 All samples north of Tropic of Cancer. This would include defined samples of U.S. Caucasians, African Americans and Hispanics and NCBI|NIHPDR.
10	CENTRAL/SOUTH AMERICA	\N	 Samples from Mainland Central and South America, Island Nations of western Atlantic, Gulf of Mexico and Eastern Pacific.
11	UNKNOWN	\N	 Samples with unknown geographic provenience that are not global in nature.
